# claude-mgr вАФ project context for Claude Code sessions

A **read-mostly governance CLI** for the user's large Claude Code harness (inventory / conflicts / `config show-effective` / doctor / snapshot-rollback / remove-update). Zero-runtime-dependency Node ESM, Windows-hardened, **dry-run-by-default**, lives OUTSIDE Claude Code's loader. The user is a non-coder ("vibe coding") вАФ reply in Chinese.

## Per-Unit Definition of Done (every work unit, in order)
1. **Regression** вАФ full `node --test` green, no regressions.
2. **Code review** вАФ a SEPARATE `code-reviewer` pass (never self-approve); fix Blocker/High before commit.
3. **Boundary** вАФ edge cases covered (use the `test/fixtures/` corpus: broken / unicode-paths / long-paths / case-insensitive / вА¶).
4. **Acceptance** вАФ falsifiable criterion (golden-file oracle; "matches golden", never "exit 0").
5. **Git** вАФ commit on green; **one file = one commit** (data fixtures may commit per-category); push.

## Environment gotchas (verified on this machine)
- Node **v24.14.0**; runner = `node --test` (zero deps). Run from the repo root.
- The **PowerShell tool is unreliable here** вЖТ use the **Bash tool with POSIX paths** (`/c/Dev/Projects/claude-mgr`).
- Windows **Developer Mode is ON** вЖТ the dogfood symlink uses `cmd /c mklink /D` (PowerShell `New-Item -SymbolicLink` fails).
- **Subagents may TIME OUT on long tasks here вАФ but do NOT disable/abandon delegation.** The DoD's SEPARATE `code-reviewer` and `executor` passes MUST stay delegated (never self-author + self-approve вАФ that gate is the whole point). Mitigate timeouts by scoping each delegated task SMALL (one sub-unit at a time) and **resuming/retrying** a timed-out agent; fall back to a direct Edit ONLY for a tiny fix a reviewer has already prescribed.
- The tool resolves the governed `~/.claude/` and `~/.claude/hooks/lib` via the home dir вАФ **independent of cwd**, so develop here, not inside `~/.claude/`.
- GitHub remote: `exampleuser-jpg/claude-mgr` (PRIVATE), `main` вЖТ `origin/main`.
